  <raw>-SUZUKI REPORTS INCREASE IN 2010 GLOBAL AUTOMOBILE SALES VOLUME FIGURES




ENP Newswire - 28 February 2011 

Release date- 24022011 - HAMAMATSU, Japan - Suzuki Motor Corporation is pleased to announce that the company has achieved an increase in global automobile sales volume - 2,589 thousand units (112% year-over-year) - for the first time in three years. The growth is attributed to increases in the Asian market, particularly India, according to Takashi Iwatsuki, Deputy Executive General Manager, Global Marketing, Suzuki Motor Corportation. 



Japan - The sales volume remained the same as the previous year. The market slowdown after October was due to the termination of government subsidies for eco-friendly car purchases. However, the new Swift contributed with an increase of sales. 
Europe -- The sales volume decreased year-over-year owing to the market slowdown after the termination of the car scrapping scheme of each government, as well as a sales decline by the influence of exchange rates. 
Asia - The sales volume in Asia, except Japan, increases year-over year thanks to increased sales in India. 

SMC Automobile Sales Volume (thousand units) 

Japan sales volume 625 (100%) 

Overseas sales volume 1,964 (117%) 

(except Japan) 

Europe 243 (84%) 

Asia* 1,540 (127%) 

Others 181 (96%) 

Global sales volume 2,589 (112%) 

*also includes China and India 

About Suzuki 
The Brea, Calif.-based Operations of American Suzuki Motor Corporation (ASMC) was founded in 1963 by parent company Suzuki Motor Corporation (SMC) and currently markets its vehicles in the United States through a network of approximately 300 automotive dealerships and numerous other motorcycle, ATV and marine distributors in 49 states. With global headquarters in Hamamatsu, Japan, SMC is a diversified worldwide automobile, motorcycle, and outboard motor manufacturer. In 2010, SMC sold more than 2.5 million new cars and trucks and more than 2.8 million motorcycles and ATVs. Founded in 1909 and incorporated in 1920, SMC has operations in 196 countries and regions. For more information, visit www.media.suzukiauto.com. Suzuki can also be found on Twitter (@SuzukiAuto), Facebook (www.Facebook.com/SuzukiAuto) and YouTube (www.YouTube.com/SuzukiAutomotive). 

# # # 

Media Contacts 

Jeff Holland, American Suzuki - (714) 996-7040 ext. 2464, jeff.holland@suz.com 

Shamit Choksey, American Suzuki - (714) 996-7040 ext. 2255, shamit.choksey@suz.com 

[Editorial queries for this story should be sent to newswire@enpublishing.co.uk ]</raw>
